### [183] [Beltrami coefficient and angular distortion of discrete geometric mappings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19240)
*Zhiyuan Lyu,Gary P. T. Choi*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 该论文建立了角畸变与Beltrami系数之间的理论联系，为量化表面映射算法质量提供了新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 几何映射在科学与工程中广泛应用，保角性是其重要质量指标。现有研究分别关注角畸变和Beltrami系数作为保角性度量，但两者之间的精确关系尚未被系统分析。

Method: 通过理论分析建立角畸变与Beltrami系数之间的数学关系，推导出Beltrami系数范数与三角形元素绝对角畸变的简单关系式，并提出用Beltrami系数估计最大角畸变的公式。通过数值实验验证理论结果，涵盖保角映射、拟保角映射和保面积映射算法。

Result: 发现了Beltrami系数范数与映射下三角形元素绝对角畸变之间的简单关系，建立了用Beltrami系数估计最大角畸变的公式。数值实验在生物学和工程学的多种表面网格上验证了理论结果的正确性。

Conclusion: 通过建立角畸变与Beltrami系数之间的理论基础，为表面映射算法的量化分析开辟了新途径，提供了更精确的保角性评估方法。

Abstract: Over the past several decades, geometric mapping methods have been extensively developed and utilized for many practical problems in science and engineering. To assess the quality of geometric mappings, one common consideration is their conformality. In particular, it is well-known that conformal mappings preserve angles and hence the local geometry, which is beneficial in many applications. Therefore, many existing works have focused on the angular distortion as a measure of the conformality of mappings. More recently, quasi-conformal theory has attracted increasing attention in the development of geometric mapping methods, in which the Beltrami coefficient has also been considered as a representation of the conformal distortion. However, the precise connection between these two concepts has not been analyzed. In this work, we study the connection between the two concepts and establish a series of theoretical results. In particular, we discover a simple relationship between the norm of the Beltrami coefficient of a mapping and the absolute angular distortion of triangle elements under the mapping. We can further estimate the maximal angular distortion using a simple formula in terms of the Beltrami coefficient. We verify the developed theoretical results and estimates using numerical experiments on multiple geometric mapping methods, covering conformal mapping, quasi-conformal mapping, and area-preserving mapping algorithms, for a variety of surface meshes in biology and engineering. Altogether, by establishing the theoretical foundation for the relationship between the angular distortion and Beltrami coefficient, our work opens up new avenues for the quantification and analysis of surface mapping algorithms.

</details>

### [184] [Linear Social Choice with Few Queries: A Moment-Based Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19510)
*Luise Ge,Daniel Halpern,Gregory Kehne,Yevgeniy Vorobeychik*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 研究在极端通信预算下的社会选择问题，通过建模选民类型分布并恢复其矩作为候选选择的统计摘要，证明每个选民只需1-2次成对比较即可实现社会福利最大化并识别分布矩


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前社会选择规则通常假设获得完整排序，而实际对齐实践虽然追求多样性，却将选民视为匿名且比较独立，每个选民仅提取约1比特信息。这促使研究在极端通信预算下的社会选择问题，以弥合理论与实践的差距

Method: 在线性社会选择模型中，将选民效用建模为潜在选民类型与候选嵌入的内积。将选民群体建模为未知的选民类型分布，通过恢复其矩作为候选选择的统计摘要。分析不同查询方式（成对比较、分级比较）对矩识别的能力

Result: 证明每个选民只需一次成对比较即可选择最大化社会福利的候选，但无法识别二阶矩；每个选民两次成对比较或一次分级比较可识别二阶矩及所有高阶矩，从而完全恢复选民类型分布

Conclusion: 在极端通信预算下，通过矩恢复方法可实现高效的社会选择，支持包括不平等感知福利标准在内的多种社会选择目标，为实际对齐实践提供了理论框架

Abstract: Most social choice rules assume access to full rankings, while current alignment practice -- despite aiming for diversity -- typically treats voters as anonymous and comparisons as independent, effectively extracting only about one bit per voter. Motivated by this gap, we study social choice under an extreme communication budget in the linear social choice model, where each voter's utility is the inner product between a latent voter type and the embedding of the context and candidate. The candidate and voter spaces may be very large or even infinite. Our core idea is to model the electorate as an unknown distribution over voter types and to recover its moments as informative summary statistics for candidate selection. We show that one pairwise comparison per voter already suffices to select a candidate that maximizes social welfare, but this elicitation cannot identify the second moment and therefore cannot support objectives that account for inequality. We prove that two pairwise comparisons per voter, or alternatively a single graded comparison, identify the second moment; moreover, these richer queries suffice to identify all moments, and hence the entire voter-type distribution. These results enable principled solutions to a range of social choice objectives including inequality-aware welfare criteria such as taking into account the spread of voter utilities and choosing a representative subset.

</details>


### [185] [Envy-Free School Redistricting Between Two Groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19701)
*Daisuke Shibatani,Yutaro Yamaguchi*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 研究将公平分配理论应用于学区重划，针对两个群体情况，提出1-松弛嫉妒自由概念，证明其存在性并给出多项式时间算法


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究显示，对于三个或更多群体，需要添加o(n)额外座位才能获得几乎无嫉妒分配，这在实践中难以实现。本文聚焦于两个群体的特殊情况，探索更实用的公平分配方案

Method: 引入1-松弛嫉妒自由概念，限制每个学校的容量违反不超过1个座位（而非总量限制）。证明对于两个群体，总是存在这样的分配，并提供多项式时间算法来寻找这种分配

Result: 证明对于两个群体，总是存在1-松弛嫉妒自由分配，且可以在多项式时间内找到。这与三个或更多群体需要大量额外座位的情况形成对比

Conclusion: 对于两个群体的学区重划问题，1-松弛嫉妒自由提供了实用且可实现的公平分配方案，相比先前研究的理论保证更具实践可行性

Abstract: We study an application of fair division theory to school redistricting. Procaccia, Robinson, and Tucker-Foltz (SODA 2024) recently proposed a mathematical model to generate redistricting plans that provide theoretically guaranteed fairness among demographic groups of students. They showed that an almost proportional allocation can be found by adding $O(g \log g)$ extra seats in total, where $g$ is the number of groups. In contrast, for three or more groups, adding $o(n)$ extra seats is not sufficient to obtain an almost envy-free allocation in general, where $n$ is the total number of students. In this paper, we focus on the case of two groups. We introduce a relevant relaxation of envy-freeness, termed 1-relaxed envy-freeness, which limits the capacity violation not in total but at each school to at most one. We show that there always exists a 1-relaxed envy-free allocation, which can be found in polynomial time.

</details>


### [186] [Just-in-Time Resale in an Ahead-of-Time Auction: An Event Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.20175)
*Burak Öz,Christoph Schlegel,Akaki Mamageishvili*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 研究Arbitrum的Timeboost机制在主要用户采用Kairos后的变化，发现二级市场出现导致一级拍卖竞争显著下降，Arbitrum收益减少，一级拍卖失去有效的价值提取功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二级即时市场（Kairos）的出现如何影响Arbitrum Timeboost机制中提前拍卖的动态，特别是对一级拍卖竞争和收益分配的影响。

Method: 分析Arbitrum Timeboost机制在主要用户（Wintermute和Selini Capital）采用Kairos前后的数据变化，比较一级拍卖的竞争程度、支付比例和收益分配。

Result: 一级拍卖竞争显著下降，Arbitrum收益减少：Kairos采用后，一级拍卖支付仅占最高出价的14.8%（之前为62.7%），搜索者利润份额降低。尽管总利润规模相似，但一级拍卖失去价值提取功能。二级市场（Kairos）捕获了大部分价值。

Conclusion: 二级市场的出现削弱了一级拍卖的价值提取能力，Arbitrum需要修改拍卖设计来重新捕获价值，包括减少价值与支付之间的差距，采用动态保留价格等策略。

Abstract: We study Arbitrum's Timeboost mechanism following the adoption of Kairos by its main users -- Wintermute and Selini Capital -- to understand how the emergence of a just-in-time secondary market affects the dynamics of an ahead-of-time primary auction. We find that competition in the primary auction significantly declines and surplus shifts away from Arbitrum. After the transition, bids paid in the primary auction correspond to only 14.8\% of the highest bid (compared to nearly 62.7\% in the \textit{Pre-Kairos} era), and a lower share of searcher profit-and-loss (PnL), despite total PnL (gross of auction payments) remains of similar magnitude across regimes. This indicates that the primary auction effectively ceases to function as a meaningful surplus extraction mechanism. Although demand for time-boosting valuable CEX--DEX arbitrage transactions continues to increase with external price volatility, observed bids in the Timeboost auction no longer reflect this demand. While the exact distribution of the additional value between searchers and Kairos remains unclear, the evidence suggests that the secondary market captures a substantial share at the expense of the primary auctioneer. We conclude by outlining possible ways for Arbitrum to recapture this value, including modifying the auction design to reduce the gap between value and payments and adopting a dynamic reserve price.

</details>

### [187] [Nonlinear Flexibility Effects on Flight Dynamics of High-Aspect-Ratio Wings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19725)
*Nikolaos D. Tantaroudas,Andrea Da Ronch,Ilias Karachalios,Kenneth J. Badcock,Rafael Palacios*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 研究几何非线性和结构柔性对高展弦比机翼飞行动力学的影响，开发了气动弹性-飞行动力学耦合框架，通过参数化研究量化了柔性对配平、颤振和阵风响应的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高海拔长航时飞机通常采用高展弦比机翼，这类机翼具有显著的几何非线性和结构柔性，传统线性分析方法可能无法准确预测其飞行动力学特性，需要开发能够处理强耦合效应的分析框架。

Method: 开发了气动弹性-飞行动力学耦合框架：1) 采用几何精确梁理论描述结构；2) 使用非定常二维条带理论计算气动力；3) 基于四元数的刚体运动方程描述飞行动力学；4) 三个子系统通过载荷和运动传递在每个时间步进行整体耦合；5) 通过系统参数化研究，改变机翼刚度参数（跨越多个数量级）。

Result: 1) 增加柔性会根本改变配平条件、颤振边界和动态阵风响应；2) 大静态变形产生有效上反角，改变升力方向并需要更高的配平攻角；3) 长周期模态在高柔性水平下失稳；4) 颤振速度随刚度参数降低而显著退化；5) 框架验证显示与已发表基准在固有频率、颤振速度和非线性静态变形方面吻合良好。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了关于何时线性分析可接受、何时需要完全耦合非线性工具的定量指导，强调了在高柔性配置中正确考虑预应力平衡的重要性，为高展弦比机翼设计提供了重要分析工具。

Abstract: This paper investigates the effects of geometric nonlinearity and structural flexibility on the flight dynamics of high-aspect-ratio wings representative of high-altitude long endurance aircraft configurations. A coupled aeroelastic flight dynamic framework is developed, combining a geometrically exact beam formulation for the structure, unsteady two-dimensional strip theory for the aerodynamics, and quaternion-based rigid-body equations for the flight dynamics. The three subsystems are monolithically coupled through consistent load and motion transfer at each time step. A systematic parametric study is conducted by varying the wing stiffness across several orders of magnitude, spanning from nearly rigid to very flexible configurations. The study reveals that increasing flexibility fundamentally alters trim conditions, flutter boundaries, and dynamic gust response. In particular, large static deformations create an effective dihedral that modifies the lift direction and necessitates higher trim angles of attack. The phugoid mode is shown to destabilise at high flexibility levels, consistent with findings in the literature. Flutter speed degradation is quantified as a function of the stiffness parameter, showing significant reductions for very flexible configurations when the pre-stressed equilibrium is correctly accounted for. The framework is validated against published aircraft benchmarks, demonstrating good agreement in natural frequencies, flutter speeds, and nonlinear static deflections. Results provide quantitative guidance on when linear analysis is acceptable and when fully coupled nonlinear tools become essential.

</details>


### [188] [A computational framework to predict the spreading of Alzheimer's disease](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19829)
*A. Vazquez-Palomo,C. Betegón,J. Weickenmeier,E. Martínez-Pañeda*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 开发了一个三维有限元计算框架，结合多蛋白传输和脑组织变形，在解剖学真实几何中模拟阿尔茨海默病进展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解微观蛋白质动力学如何转化为宏观组织退化是阿尔茨海默病研究的主要挑战，需要将蛋白质传播与脑萎缩联系起来。

Method: 使用反应-扩散方程（Fisher-Kolmogorov类型）描述tau和β-淀粉样蛋白的传播，结合朊病毒样生长机制和白质纤维束的各向异性传输；通过超弹性本构模型表示蛋白质依赖性体积损失引起的脑萎缩；开发自动化预处理流程生成有限元网格并从医学影像数据重建轴突取向场。

Result: 模型重现了阿尔茨海默病的关键形态学模式，与纵向成像测量结果显示出良好的定量一致性。

Conclusion: 该框架为研究阿尔茨海默病进展提供了一个可扩展的计算平台，模型和图像处理框架已开源供研究使用。

Abstract: Alzheimer's disease is characterised by the spreading of misfolded proteins and progressive structural changes in the brain. Despite significant clinical research, understanding how microscopic protein dynamics translate into macroscopic tissue degeneration remains a major challenge. In this work, we present a three-dimensional, finite element-based computational framework to model disease progression by combining multi-protein transport and brain tissue deformation within anatomically realistic geometries. The propagation of toxic tau and amyloid-beta proteins is described using reaction-diffusion equations of the Fisher-Kolmogorov type, incorporating prion-like growth mechanisms and anisotropic transport along white matter fibre tracts. Brain atrophy is represented through a hyperelastic constitutive model driven by protein-dependent volume loss. Subject-specific simulations are achieved through an automated preprocessing pipeline that generates finite element meshes and reconstructs axonal orientation fields from medical imaging data. The model reproduces key morphological patterns observed in Alzheimer's disease and shows good quantitative agreement with longitudinal imaging measurements. Overall, the proposed framework offers an extensible computational platform for studying Alzheimer's disease progression across subject-specific brain geometries. The models developed, including the image processing framework (BrainImage2Mesh) and the coupled bio-chemo-mechanical COMSOL finite element implementation, are made freely available to download at https://mechmat.web.ox.ac.uk/codes.

</details>
